
-----title
台州 (出生地)

id='poem_sentence_1_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124681'>百夫不当十，一夫费千镮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124681'>恐被<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤集作彼）</span>嗜利徒，无能御国患。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124681'>老母与少妇，蓬头走江干。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124681'>挽之不得留，悲泣声彻天。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124681'>母曰我壮子，妇曰我健夫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124681'>衣裳破无补，田园荒未锄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124681'>一朝弃我去，饥寒我何如。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124681'>抑恐惰军气，累汝重汝辜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124681'>今业已分离，把袂略须臾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124590_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124589?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124589'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124589'>女萝去长松，藉藉纷委地。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124589'>矇瞍辞诏相，十步九颠踬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124589'>弱昧惭陋质，先生未终弃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124589'>再拜愿有闻，服膺敢失坠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124588'>三年在门墙，一日泣岐路。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124588'>窗前长新绿，生意自呈露。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124588'>愿君日强饭，安排济时具。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124626'>到手功名还漫浪，褆身德业念居诸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124626_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124615?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_124615'>思昔汉中殆，羯奴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>自荒逖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124615'>驱侵警边陲，腥臊污<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>华国。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124615'>官守蒙胡尘<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作既蒙尘，据明本改）</span>，宫庙入胡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>域。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124615'>奸回执国命，地土轻弃掷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124615'>倒悬头足互，妖氛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>日月黑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124615'>念之不忍言，言之泪沾臆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124615'>寿皇雄武姿，一洗曾莫得。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124615'>似闻元戎已启行，官军所到无勍敌。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124615'>倒戈横尸四十里，搴旗获马六千匹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124615'>长安遗老今尚在，壶浆筐篚输悃愊。<div id='poem_sentence_19_124615'>胡憯不念涵煦恩，坐看行人斗道侧。<div id='poem_sentence_19_124615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_124615'>嗟予少小则古昔，有志未就苦弱植。<div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_124684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124684'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124684'>一树栖残雪，不禁春夜霜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124684'>香飘非宝篆，粉褪厌时妆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124684'>且合收馀白，应难待晚黄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124684'>自便篱落好，榛棘不相妨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124684'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_124684_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124682")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124682'>凄其望云汉，旱饥何频年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124682'>去岁秋后雨，沟壑仅少年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124682'>春耕问菑畬，馌妇多嘉言。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124682'>夏耘喜优渥，驿驿生翠烟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124682'>不雨宁几日，已复忧亏愆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124682'>伤弓慨心事，过计乃不然。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124682'>风雷变俄顷，肤寸速九天。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124682'>夜坐听倾倒，朝起望渺绵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124682'>时哉此甘霔，不后亦不先。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124682'>我无负郭资，墨突非所怜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124682'>但愿时丰登，有粟均里廛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124682'>岁晚称寿觞，一笑生春妍。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124682'>彼苍其或者，副此心拳拳。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124682'>拜赐盈百室，敬诵良耜篇。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_124682_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己卯夏忧雨偶作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124604")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124604'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124604'>昨者忧不足，今者厌有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124604'>垂垂匝晓夕，滟滟平浍渠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124604'>苗事方用壮，过潦非所虞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124604'>但虑盈与亏，理或相乘除。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124604'>它日傥望霓，神贶俱堕虚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124604'>造物愿有终，屯膏时其输。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124604'>自此大有年，大书不一书。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124604'>饱饭乐田社，一官徒区区。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124604'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_124604_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闲行溪西得梅数花喜甚偶成小诗呈诸赵兄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124639")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124639'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124639'>作意每不偶，邂逅与心会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124639'>畴昔问寒梅，李园不成醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124639'>今夕亦何夕，见此万花最。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124639'>独立如高人，凛凛尘世外。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124639'>藤藓半侵剥，风雪几颠沛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124639'>蕞尔篱落间，劲气夺松桧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124639'>下视桃李场，碌碌千百辈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124639'>古淡不入眼，何能供世嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124639'>苦心抱岁寒，天其知我矣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124639'>此行得此花，嶷然为增气。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124639'>置之几席间，相对喜不寐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124639'>有果硕不食，明朝日南至。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124639'>芽檗或未知，尔乃太蚤计。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124639'>三嗅味清绝，令人发长喟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124639'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_124639_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方山和篇再和韵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124611")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124611_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_124611_0'>① 方山叔祖讳知仁，字仁仲，文公门人</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124611'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124611'>慇勤里社间，谈笑文字会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124611'>平生一尊酒，无虑千百醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124611'>问梅穷涧冈，乐事此其最。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124611'>风霜尽木末，冰雪封户外。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124611'>谁其念岑寂，自得以颠沛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124611'>岁寒二三友，已不数苍桧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124611'>卓彼方山翁，自许行偕<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤集作出行）</span>辈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124611'>古心味玄酒，于世百不嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124611'>少小诵佳篇，搜句亦奇伟<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作矣，据名贤集改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124611'>年来久不作，吾党几丧气。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124611'>珠璧忽堕前，畴昔曾梦寐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124611'>三咏结束语，坐令百感至。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124611'>来者恐未然，往者非所计。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124611'>汗青几名节，徒起千载喟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124611'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_124611_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方山有求转语之作并用韵二章<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124610")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124610'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124610'>观物非外索，具眼以心会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124610'>微阳花病槁，宁供等闲醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124610'>我尝课前作，无言乃为最。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124610'>譬彼清庙瑟，一唱弦越外。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124610'>万卉染春色，生意岂不沛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124610'>何物漏天机，一点映寒桧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124610'>我欲屋溪曲，种竹十数辈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124610'>疏影浸清浅，作此苦淡嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124610'>方山于此花，论交亦久矣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124610'>憔悴对冰雪，中有盖世气。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124610'>向来多朋从，痛饮忘夜寐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124610'>旧事俱已非，尚善诗押至。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124610'>俯就相唱酬，殆为后来计。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124610'>一花未足多，夫子亦何喟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124610'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_124610_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124609?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124609'>四时冬复春，造化一机会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124609'>朔风空草木，馀蘖犹病醉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124609'>梅花于其间，居殿复居最。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124609'>三春在何许，不在粉须外。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124609'>我尝玩兹理，若决江河沛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124609'>冰壑卧寒松，雪岭立老桧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124609'>见命谓受独，落落一二辈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124609'>有此不改节，不与世同嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124609'>抱贞开化元，此花而已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124609'>整刷此精神，寸草亦生气。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124609'>嗟嗟迷复者，胶轕随寤寐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124609'>萌檗寻斧斤，岂知七日至。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124609'>击壤咏天根，巧历不能计。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124609'>持以印梅花，无语独叹喟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124609'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_124609_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div id='poem_124653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林倅到迓之途中小诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月初一）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1223年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124653'>简书奔走日冲冲，偶此郊行兴易浓。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124653'>雨意酝成春野意，云容点就晓山容。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124653'>茧丝贮色桑条上，饼饵吹香麦陇中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124653'>忽忆故园归去好，云山知隔几千重。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124653'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_124653_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124645?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_124409_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124634?labeling=true' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124634")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124634'>昔君游我里，诸老皆竞爽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124634'>今踰三十年，百事一非往。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124634'>君今来京都，相对各槁项。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124634'>清灯话畴昔，未语意先惘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124634'>橐中剩缃帙，挈来耀书榥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124634'>栒虡列群编，金石振逸响。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124634'>又如春水阔，縠澜敷浩瀁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124634'>绣鞶饫耳闻，锦囊惬心赏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124634'>今夕亦何夕，尘塞为披敞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124634'>吾衰亦久矣，欲勉不可强。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124634'>尚记诸老言，种收同卤莽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124634'>顾我困朝饥，羡君富秋穰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124634'>何日遂赋归，相从问陇㽘。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124634'>滞穗傥可拾，我亦歌击壤。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124538'>何人剥啄扣云关，袖有新诗数百篇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124538'>宫徵自调相和应，珠玑不拣尽光圆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124538'>昌黎荐士惭无路，东野盘空枉笑天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124538'>闻道二亲犹未葬，知谁著眼为渠怜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124538'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_124538_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>承见再和用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124536")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_124536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124536'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124536'>簇簇枝头缀浅黄，鼻通四远熟留藏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124536'>秋于对树疑添色，雨不多时怕减香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124536'>花事索人非易管，诗情得酒为新尝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124536'>丛芳德色惊人句，影下重吟驻夕阳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124536'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_124536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_124536'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_124536_0'>⑴ 原校：一本云乞将花事从君管，剩有诗情得酒尝，推桉已惊新什至，蔼如病思得春阳</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_124536_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1302807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋义约规式</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302807")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302807'>余每叹王政不行，风俗不古，无告者多，而民生重可哀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302807_comment'></div>嘉熙元年春，归自中都，得乡之义约，隐几读之，其悯穷恤死，庶几古者同井相扶持之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302807_comment'></div>坚此意，推而广之，必有闻风而来取法者，则斯约之倡，其仁遍吾邦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302807_comment'></div>余虽贫，亦愿助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302807_comment'></div>喜而为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302807_comment'></div>是岁夏重午前十日，杜某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1302807_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋项文卿孝行录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302808")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302808'>余尚记三十年前，项君文卿馆于余族，与余兄弟交知，其为时文师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302808_comment'></div>余读是书，凡古人孝悌言行蒐辑无遗，且闻其事死如事生，将终身焉，余始知其为笃行君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302808_comment'></div>时文以钓利禄，得不得命也，而率以隳行丧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302808_comment'></div>孝悌之道，天理根之以生，人极因之以立，充之足以为尧舜，违之不足以为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302808_comment'></div>人而从事于斯，时文盖不足言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302808_comment'></div>微是书，几失吾文卿，为之掩卷，抆泪自痛，不惟有愧古人，其有愧于文卿多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1302808_comment'></div>使家有是书，熟玩而深体之，则消暴慢之气，长顺睦之风，人伦其有不厚，教化其有不美耶？</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1302808_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋林逢吉晦翁二帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302809")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302809'>康吉堂富藏古贤名帖，而于文公二帖，尤所珍爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302809_comment'></div>世之尚异挟奇，借耳目之玩者，决不解此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302809_comment'></div>余观轴尾所志，考订绍兴事为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302809_comment'></div>公之前帖殆可句释，不得不然之论，言巽而旨微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302809_comment'></div>后帖莫知何时，有党无党，所不敢闻，细玩斯语，其关于世道，尤可深慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302809_comment'></div>逢吉珍爱此帖，更为予订之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1302809_comment'></div>嘉熙元年夏五至日，杜某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1302809_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车隘轩闲居录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302802")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302802'>自中朝文物之盛播于东南，吾乡俊秀能文之士在在不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302802_comment'></div>幸而登上第、骋荣途者百不一二，不幸而陆沉约处、首白衣褐者，可伛指枚数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302802_comment'></div>夫能不能，才也，遇不遇，命也，而闭门挟策，隐几著书，矻矻穷年，抱其所有，曾不少槩见者，可胜慨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302802_comment'></div>嘉熙改元之春，余归自中都，车君若水袖其祖隘轩《閒居录》访余于穷阎之下，既而又得其小藁读之，得陈筼窗之序读之，于是隘轩之文叠卷累帙，铿鍧炳耀，殆与插架名编濯濯争丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302802_comment'></div>《閒居录》盖公自志其平日所得，而若水又搜采旧闻，饰而附益焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302802_comment'></div>其释经评史，确古商今，不袭传记之旧说、简策之陈言，迥出新意，自成一家议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1302802_comment'></div>亦尝熟阅而细考之，如邪正义利雅俗之杂，与傲下谄上、凌弱畏势等语，诚不易之确论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1302802_comment'></div>至谓以僻异解经，当与侮圣言同科，尤见其所守条律断断严甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1302802_comment'></div>然毋友不如己之说、昔在帝尧之说、尚书之说、卑服之说，若此之类，则余所未解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1302802_comment'></div>余距隘轩之居一舍而近，读其文，想其人，乃昉乎此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1302802_comment'></div>因自恨余之甚陋于闻，尤恨不及见公，质其所未解，而终陋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1302802_comment'></div>昔王氏《中说》，其格言雅训，可以上续七篇之书，而后世乃或致疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1302802_comment'></div>其间谓独其家以为名世，外人皆莫之知，李习之仅以比《太公家教》尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1302802_comment'></div>至近世大儒以隐君子目之，而后千古之是非始定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1302802_comment'></div>嗟夫，立言之难也若此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1302802_comment'></div>盖其名位不列于仕，功状不登于史，道德不称于其徒，福畤辈不能收坠缉散，阐而彰之，则所谓抱其所有，不少槩见，终泯泯于汾曲而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1302802_comment'></div>此固人之所同慨，其责宁不在为子若孙者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1302802_comment'></div>若水盖车氏之福畤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1302802_comment'></div>强请余序之，辞弗获，姑叙其略，以俟后之论定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1302802_comment'></div>隘轩名似庆，字石卿，其居黄岩邑西马家山云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1302802_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞起居郎奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302794")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302794'>臣论鸣复，未见施行，忽拜左史之命，则是所言不当，姑示优迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302794_comment'></div>臣前尝奏台谏但为仕途之捷径，初无益朝廷之纪纲，躬言之而躬蹈之，臣之罪愈大。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1302794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　杜范于家中闲居。作品：《书于立斋自戒并示诸子》、《詹世显老丈以诗送米和其韵》<div id='poem_124606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书于立斋自戒并示诸子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124606")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124606'>晦以昭明德，怯以成勇功。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124606'>用拙巧莫尚，持静动攸宗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124606'>惟柔养真刚，自下升高崇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124606'>虚可使实积，小乃与大通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124606'>守约博有归，味淡甘无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124606'>万里以是观，一心须自融。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124606'>戒哉骄与盈，外强中空空。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_124606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>詹世显老丈舂米为赠时有张老之子携其父诗求月助即以詹米转馈之詹丈以诗送米和其诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124686")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124686'>归来两见春载耜，老矣陈人愧髦士。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124686'>书生活计常若拙，瓶粟屡空固其理。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124686'>石庄好义无不为，独将饱腹念朝饥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124686'>担石赪肩米叩户，要转儿啼成欢嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124686'>此赐何敢望此老，况有新诗非草草。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124686'>再拜为之惊且惭，锦章玉粲斗新好。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124686'>我贫犹有稻粱谋，更有贫士需麦舟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124686'>为君乞与君然否，乐施曷计谁家留。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124686'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_124686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　八月，差杜范知宁国府，杜范一再请辞，不允。作品：《跋徐季节文》、《跋郑筒子求书陈情表后》、《跋薛倅漫笔》、《辞知宁国奏》、《再辞知宁国奏》<div id='poem_1302814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋徐季节文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302814")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302814'>余祖、父及乡族先辈皆季节先生弟子，余幼时已闻其笃行雅言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302814_comment'></div>虽酬对俗语，莫非师训，至今传诵，以相警厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302814_comment'></div>今其遗文仅数篇，读之使人凛凛有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302814_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302814_comment'></div>形天地间皆实理也，物不实则隳，事不实则坏，人不实则危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302814_comment'></div>公之文，公之实也，知公之为重者，可不摭其实而步趋之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1302814_comment'></div>不然，崇而衒之，夫奚益！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1302814_comment'></div>嘉熙戊戌夏六月六日，里人杜某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1302814_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋郑简子求书陈情表后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302815")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302815'>右李令伯《陈情表》，杜某为郑大惠书，书已而言曰：令伯非义不仕晋，而利禄之诱，终不足以夺其孝爱之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302815_comment'></div>吐出肺肝，字字痛恻，后之读者无不废卷兴叹，而况事有适类，情有甚同，如郑君者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302815_comment'></div>噫，令伯之陈情，令伯之不得已也，顾安知后千载而有戚戚于心，抚事悲慨，至于屡诉而不能自已者，岂昌黎公所谓「旷百世而相感，不自知其何心」者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302815_comment'></div>余既书之，又重为世之忍心背德者愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302815_comment'></div>嘉熙戊戌重午后四日识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1302815_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋薛倅漫笔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302816")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302816'>余屏居山村，耳不闻户外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302816_comment'></div>夏翼父归自东嘉，袖二车薛君诗什访余，乃知其为枢使公之令子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302816_comment'></div>赫赫钟鼎之家，乃兴入烟云，思涵月露，翛然幽人雅士之韵若是耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302816_comment'></div>金壁烂烂，置古罍洗其间，珍玩错陈，俱不俗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302816_comment'></div>余不但不能诗，亦非知诗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302816_comment'></div>秋风搜桂，夜气澄栏，命酒半觞，阅漫笔一二篇，便觉尘思辟易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1302816_comment'></div>其如别友人事，入唐人奥处，七言句格，尤多清古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1302816_comment'></div>昔人投躯破的之论，料是工夫更放精熟耳，未识知诗者以为如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1302816_comment'></div>嘉熙戊戌中秋前十日，杜某识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1302816_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9a3d254182f147028d158cd671a3c4ae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9a3d254182f147028d158cd671a3c4ae");'><span id='9a3d254182f147028d158cd671a3c4ae_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1245')">1244-1245年</a>，63-64岁</div><div id='9a3d254182f147028d158cd671a3c4ae' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　杜范于家中闲居。作品：《雪中成十一韵》<div id='poem_124678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪中成十一韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124678")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124678'>入冬多疠气，阳泄<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤集作浅）</span>月令畅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124678'>隐雷声间作，万蛰惊塞向。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124678'>数日凝重阴，云同寒威壮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124678'>飞琼遍天宇，色界铺宝藏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124678'>前此亦屡白，玉瑞此其创。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124678'>缄运孰主张，一雪压千瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124678'>纷纷富家儿，羔酒醉金帐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124678'>谁思道丐者，双脚红玳样。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124678'>顾我虽甚贫，可挟尚有纩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124678'>蚤起愿年丰，共饱拜天贶。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124678'>天意然不然，独立为楚怆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_124678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　正月，除同知枢密院事，杜范不拜。作品：《辞同知枢密奏》、《辞免新除予郡奏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　三月壬寅，诏以杜范提举洞宵宫。作品：《提举洞宵宫谢表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　十月壬辰，诏杜范提举万寿观兼侍读。作品：《辞提举万寿观兼侍读奏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　十一月辛丑，诏杜范赴职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　十二月庚午，杜范拜右丞相，兼枢密使，提举实录院，兼提举编类聖政。作品：《辞右相奏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a><div id='poem_1302840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋丘木居叶世英序后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302840")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302840'>孙真人有言：针灸之功过半于汤药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302840_comment'></div>而近世之医，往往按方言药，为灸者少，为针者又加少，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302840_comment'></div>难易之势殊，而迟速之验异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302840_comment'></div>木居谓叶兄长于针灸，岂尝读黄帝岐伯诸书，果能测经源而扶危弱者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302840_comment'></div>余非深知叶君者，以木居之言为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302840_comment'></div>淳祐甲辰重阳前一日，黄山杜某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1302840_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1302841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1302841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1302841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋郑药斋墓志<span class='inlineComment2'>（安道尊人，戴彦肃撰。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_1302841")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1302841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1302841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302841'>余不识郑君，识其子镇安道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302841_comment'></div>余甚爱安道亹亹好学，研味理奥，自拔流俗，固疑其必有家庭诗礼之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302841_comment'></div>今观彦肃之志，言其教子程律甚严，不使专业举子，且以药自名其斋，有取于修慝之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302841_comment'></div>其志尚卓矣，有是子也亦宜矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302841_comment'></div>里人杜某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1302841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　正月，杜范自家启程入觐。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4aaa2a9b4d164a659b400146481e975c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4aaa2a9b4d164a659b400146481e975c");'><span id='4aaa2a9b4d164a659b400146481e975c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>，64岁</div><div id='4aaa2a9b4d164a659b400146481e975c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>五月壬戌，杜范归殡里第。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>七月，杜范葬于本县靖乡黄杜岭之原。<br /></div>

常州

衢州

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年</a>　杜范奉檄在衢州校文。作品：《和郑府判韵》、《次宗司法云字韵》、《和郑判秋闱行》、《又和郑府判韵》、《和宗司法与府判韵》、《又用韵》、《又和郑府判侯字韵》、《复用韵以见别情》、《次郑府判金字韵》<div id='poem_124647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和郑府判韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28665, "南宋", "杜范", "poem_title_124647")'>杜范</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124647'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124647'>万里扶摇整飞翮，自是凌云九霄客。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124647'>黄槐白纻秋风高，借君弹压添颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124647'>奉檄校文真误推，多才视我蚿与夔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124647'>竭力讵敢辞钝迟，寒芒在上方辉辉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124647'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_124647_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_124622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_124622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/124622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次宗司法云字韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124622'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124622'>我来縠水偿披云，秋堂霭霭生春薰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124622'>落笔盘空斗神速，刮眼一破平生闻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124622'>自笑黏黐日凭案，抽思索句曾未半。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124622'>弱步何由附天骥，肝胆轮囷惭寸管。<div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_124646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124646'>秋云黄，日月忙，登选才俊收词章。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124646'>操觚搦翰换钟鼎，往往冰炭交中肠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124646'>柯山多士称海内，勇气洗尽古战场。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124646'>笑挥笔阵示整暇，洒洒胸中书传香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124646'>此邦昔日龙头客，前后相辉九霄翮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124646'>山川孕秀不乏人，想已津津动颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124646'>题舆左岳得儒英，行整速步趋天庭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124646'>金薤琳琅耀光彩，不学砌下寒蛩鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124646'>我昔贫困如匡衡，邻灯夜照心峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124646'>区区薄宦亦谩尔，役役尘埃愧此生。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124646'>浅学幽深虽未烛，到耳独能辨丝竹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124646'>从今著意听文鸣，会使嘤嘤出幽谷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_124646_comment'></div></div></div><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_554050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_554050'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_554050'>荆璞照耀非常珍，天衢整步凌通津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_554050'>与人轩辟破畦畛，满怀拍拍无非春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_554050'>我如枥骥异远道，志在千里身未到。<div id='poem_sentence_2_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_554050'>朅来此地寻文盟，平生心事为倾倒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_554050'>饱德醉义乐有馀，况有兰玉芬庭除。<div id='poem_sentence_4_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_554050'>谐笑云云殊未厌，盘飧夜半劳兵厨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_554050'>依依此情那忍去，自恨尘鞍难久驻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_554050'>伫看飞诏自天来，殿前剩作摩空赋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_554050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 义乌

class='inlineComment2'>（名贤集作招）</span>潮厌鲜美，望水快珍脆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124633'>朅来双溪上，河鱼仅青鲤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124633'>泥滓渍肤肉，强食辄三哕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124633'>此物从何来，对之惊且喜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124633'>虽然馁败质，尚馀江海味。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124633'>令人忆故乡，沽酒为一醉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_124640'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_124640'>虞夏几百载，继以周礼乐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124640'>洋洋雅颂音，后亡前亦<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤集作世谁能）</span>作。<div id='poem_sentence_1_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_124640'>井疆贫富均，薄海咏康乐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_124640'>姬公同圣贤，积累亦不薄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124640'>宁知不数传，板荡已非昨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124640'>丘赋鲁史书，田畴郑谤作。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124640'>滕君谩忧勤，毕战空唯诺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124640'>盛古犹有憾，此岂易商榷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124640'>矧今千载后，而欲强复剥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124640'>州县工罟阱，黔黎惴沟壑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124640'>世道日浇讹，禁厉不可缚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_124640'>我尝三太息，浮云翳碧落。<div id='poem_sentence_12_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_124640'>为贫走尘埃，岂解拯民瘼。<div id='poem_sentence_13_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_124640'>州家轻任使，千钧委羸恶。<div id='poem_sentence_14_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_124640'>劳瘁敢自爱，恐负此邦托。<div id='poem_sentence_15_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_124640'>仁政安在哉，名是意已错。<div id='poem_sentence_16_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_124640'>治道去泰甚，此论东州确。<div id='poem_sentence_17_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_124640'>人言宽一分，所望恕且约。<div id='poem_sentence_18_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_124640'>一分宽未易，十分扰已博。<div id='poem_sentence_19_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_124640'>我把七篇书，人笑谓迂学。<div id='poem_sentence_22_124640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_554049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_554049'>古道湮不续，遗直声以彰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_554049'>良药见谓苦，不试徒有方。<div id='poem_sentence_1_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_554049'>岂其盖世名，可浣忧国肠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_554049'>视天方梦梦，令人歌慨慷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_554049'>心理同一辙，世学何多门。<div id='poem_sentence_4_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_554049'>倡徒各有植，成性非两存。<div id='poem_sentence_5_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_554049'>习之到圣处，心小道自尊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_554049'>工夫未易熟，毁誉何足论。<div id='poem_sentence_7_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_554049'>空言漫浩渺，实行较分寸。<div id='poem_sentence_8_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_554049'>为官志何在，监州民可问。<div id='poem_sentence_9_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_554049'>以此百纸忠，解彼千里愠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_554049'>有守矧更贤，往哉同令闻。<div id='poem_sentence_11_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_554049'>菜畦绝夜雨，麦垄摇春风。<div id='poem_sentence_12_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_554049'>板舆奉欢笑，意与物态同。<div id='poem_sentence_13_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_554049'>路才百里近，水可一夕通。<div id='poem_sentence_14_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_554049'>君其戒徒御，驾言无匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_15_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_554049'>义交味逾淡，心敬迹自疏。<div id='poem_sentence_16_554049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_554049'>球玉世所贵，车马人交趋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124651'>士有当世志，谁肯专诗名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_124651'>自古巧文字，与道关废兴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124651'>目中无全牛，肯綮技未经。<div id='poem_sentence_3_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_124651'>胡为趁风月，候虫相与鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124651'>静夜诵佳什，泠然如梦醒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124651'>瘦语自腴泽，险句自稳平。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_124651'>譬彼有源水，随流作幽清。<div id='poem_sentence_7_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_124651'>奇抱叹皓首，败屋挑寒灯。<div id='poem_sentence_8_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_124651'>天运岂其然，人力非所能。<div id='poem_sentence_9_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_124651'>我读渊明诗，悠悠千古情。<div id='poem_sentence_10_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_124651'>衔觞岂好饮，采菊非餐英。<div id='poem_sentence_11_124651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_124650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_124650'>泛观疑自戾，反视不失平。<div id='poem_sentence_6_124650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1302805'>国家中兴，爱养人才，至淳熙间，名贤彬彬辈出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1302805_comment'></div>公上接流绪，下植风声，汲沈振滞，寸善不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1302805_comment'></div>今读此编，群才毕萃，何其盛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1302805_comment'></div>自公云亡，诸老亦相继凋落，公所荐引者，其显用十无一二，而时事日新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1302805_comment'></div>由公而前若此，由公而后又若此，然则公之云亡，盖实关于世道之一变也，为之掩卷太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1302805_comment'></div>癸巳季秋二十七日。</div><div
